<script>
function ajaxsession ()
{ 
return;
var id_frs = 'a';
$.ajax({
type: 'POST',
url: "ajaxsession.php",
data: {id_frs: id_frs },
success: function(msg){
//alert(msg);
 if(msg ==1)
 {
 window.location.href="erreur.php";
 }
 if(msg ==2)
 {
window.location.href="login.php?mes=1";
 }
 if(msg ==3)
 {
 window.location.href="login.php";
 }
 setTimeout('ajaxsession()',1000);
 // parent.dhxWins.window('w1').close();
 }
});
}
</script>

function load_player(name_channel,streamer_channel)
{


if((parent.compte_type!='premium')&&(streamer_channel==''))
{
alert('Access premium required !');
return ;
}
	
	
	
	if(name_channel!='teledunet_tv')
{
//if(parent.id_membre_connected=='moderateur')alert(name_channel);
if((parent.id_membre_connected=='')||(parent.id_membre_connected.toLowerCase()=='visiteur'))
{
alert('Please connect to watch channels !');
return ;
}
}


curent_name_channel=name_channel;
curent_streamer_channel=streamer_channel;
streamer_channel=streamer_channel.replace('127.0.0.1',document.domain);
try{play_pause(true,false);}catch(err){}

try{
parent.load_js_page('http://www.teledunet.com/record_session.php?id='+(new Date().getTime())+'&channel='+name_channel,function(){parent.get_who_watch_channel(name_channel);});
}catch(err){}


first_load=false;
	var aut='?id0=';
	
		
	
	
	
			
	if(name_channel=='teledunet_tv')
	{
  jwplayer('mediaspace').setup({
    'flashplayer': 'http://www.teledunet.com/mobile/player.swf?channel='+name_channel+'&user='+parent.id_membre_connected+'&token='+parent.token,
    'id': 'playerID',
    'width': '100%',
	'height': '100%',
    'quality': 'high',
	'wmode': 'transparent',
	'provider': 'rtmp',
	'autostart': 'true',
    //'duration': '36000',
    'bufferlength': '0.1',
    'file': name_channel,
	'streamer': streamer_channel,
    'stretching': 'exactfit',
	'controlbar': 'false',
	'allowFullScreen': 'false',
  });
  
  }
  
  else
	//if(parent.id_membre_connected=='moderateur')alert(parent.access_id);
	if(streamer_channel.indexOf('rtmp://')!==0)
	{
	//alert(streamer_channel+'/'+name_channel);
	  jwplayer('mediaspace').setup({
    'flashplayer': 'http://www.teledunet.com/mobile/player.swf'+parent.access_id+'&channel='+name_channel+'&user='+parent.id_membre_connected+'&token='+parent.token,
    'id': 'playerID',
    'width': '100%',
	'height': '100%',
    'quality': 'high',
	'wmode': 'transparent',
	'provider': 'video',
	'autostart': 'true',
    //'duration': '36000',
    'bufferlength': '0.1',
    'file': streamer_channel+'/'+name_channel,
	//'streamer': streamer_channel,
    'stretching': 'exactfit',
	'controlbar': 'false',
	'allowFullScreen': 'false',
  });
	}
	else
	{
	  
  var rtmp_server=streamer_channel;
  if(server_num!=0)
  rtmp_server=server_list[server_num];
 //if(parent.id_membre_connected=='moderateur')alert(rtmp_server);
  
  jwplayer('mediaspace').setup({
    'flashplayer': 'http://www.teledunet.com/mobile/player.swf'+parent.access_id+'&channel='+name_channel+'&user='+parent.id_membre_connected+'&token='+parent.token,

    'stretching': 'exactfit',
	'controlbar': 'false',
	'allowFullScreen': 'false',
  });
 
  }
  
  player=jwplayer();
parent.player=player;
jwplayer().onIdle(function() {
		//t=setTimeout("jwplayer().play()",1000);
	t=setTimeout(function(){load_player(name_channel,streamer_channel);},1000);
	});

select_channel_playlist=function(id)
{
try
{
document.getElementById('listchaine').scrollTop=((id-1)*60)+id;
//document.body.scrollTop=0;
}catch(err){}

try
{
document.getElementById('channel_'+last_selected_channel).style.background='';
document.getElementById('td_channel_'+last_selected_channel).style.color='#000000';
document.getElementById('channel_name_'+last_selected_channel).style.color='#000000';
}catch(err){}
try
{
document.getElementById('channel_'+id).style.background='#000000';
document.getElementById('td_channel_'+id).style.color='#ffffff';
document.getElementById('channel_name_'+id).style.color='#ffffff';
document.getElementById('channel_'+id).focus();
}catch(err){}
}

format_title_page=function(s)
{
s=s.toLowerCase();
while(s.indexOf(' ')>=0)
s=s.replace(' ','_');
return s;
}

option_shift=false;
enable_shift=false;
go_shift_channel=function()
{
if(option_shift===false)return;
if(enable_shift===false)
{
document.getElementById('span_shift').style.color='#aa0000';
document.getElementById('span_live').style.color='#444444';
enable_shift=true;
name_channel=name_channel.replace('_shift','');
name_channel+='_shift';
load_player(name_channel,streamer_channel);
}
else
{
document.getElementById('span_shift').style.color='#444444';
document.getElementById('span_live').style.color='#aa0000';
enable_shift=false;

name_channel=name_channel.replace('_shift','');
//name_channel+='_shift';
load_player(name_channel,streamer_channel);
}
}

function urlencode(str) {
return str.replace('&',escape('&'));
return escape(str);
return escape(str.replace(/%/g, '%25').replace(/\+/g, '%2B')).replace(/%25/g, '%');
}
////////////////////////////
////////////////////////////
format_channel_name=function(n)
{
n=n.replace(' ','_');
n=n.replace('-','_');
return n.toLowerCase();
}

function chargerchaine(id,scroll,rtmp)
{
/////////
try{
rtmp=document.getElementById('rtmp_'+id).value;
}catch(err){}
try{
var k=on_key_board_event(id,scroll);
if(!k)return ;
}catch(err){}
/////////
/////////
/////////
if(curent_number_channel_played==id)return;
curent_number_channel_played=id;
/////////
document.getElementById('span_shift').style.color='#444444';
document.getElementById('span_live').style.color='#aa0000';
enable_shift=false;
////////
	var default_streamer='';
	name_channel=format_channel_name(document.getElementById('channel_name_'+id).innerHTML);
	if(rtmp!=undefined)
	{
	if(default_streamer=='')
	streamer_channel=rtmp.substring(0,rtmp.lastIndexOf('/'));
	else
	streamer_channel=default_streamer;
	load_player(rtmp.substring(rtmp.lastIndexOf('/')+1),streamer_channel);
	}
	else
	{
	streamer_channel=default_streamer;
	load_player(name_channel,streamer_channel);
	}


}

auto_hide_playlist=false;

show_hide_playlist_div=function(enable,w)
{
/////////////////////////

try{
document.getElementById('listchaine').focus();
window.top.document.getElementById('listchaine').focus();
}catch(err){}


width_playlist=320;
var w=get_width_window();



var h=get_height_window();


document.getElementById('listchaine').style.height=(h)+'px';

document.getElementById('listchaine').style.overflowY='auto';


//////////////////////////////////
//////////////////////////////////
//////////////////////////////////
////////////////
if(enable)
{
is_full_screen_list=true;
show_playlist(width_playlist,'relative');

try{document.getElementById('icon_site').style.visibility=affiche_top_detail?'visible':'hidden';}catch(err){};

}
else
{
is_full_screen_list=false;
document.getElementById('mediaspace').style.visibility='visible';
hide_playlist();
try{document.getElementById('icon_site').style.visibility='hidden';}catch(err){}
}
//////////////////////////////////
//////////////////////////////////
//////////////////////////////////
if(auto_hide_playlist)
{
try{clearTimeout(interval_auto_hide_playlist);}catch(err){}
interval_auto_hide_playlist=setTimeout(function(){
show_hide_playlist_div(false);
},10000);
}
//////////////////////////////////
//////////////////////////////////
//////////////////////////////////
}


show_playlist=function(w,position)
{
var w_window=get_width_window();
if(!position)position='absolute';
document.getElementById('listchaine').style.visibility='visible';
//document.getElementById('listchaine').style.position=position;

if(position=='relative')
document.getElementById('td_listchaine').style.minWidth=w+'px';



document.getElementById('listchaine').style.width=w+'px';
document.getElementById('div_masque').style.visibility='visible';
document.getElementById('div_masque').style.width=(w_window-w)+'px';
document.getElementById('div_masque').style.left=w+'px';
}

hide_playlist=function()
{
var w_window=get_width_window();

//document.getElementById('listchaine').style.position='absolute';
document.getElementById('listchaine').style.overflowY='hidden';
document.getElementById('listchaine').style.visibility='hidden';
document.getElementById('td_listchaine').style.minWidth='0px';
document.getElementById('div_masque').style.visibility='visible';
document.getElementById('div_masque').style.width=(w_window)+'px';
document.getElementById('div_masque').style.left='0px';
}

<script>

function urlencode(str) {
return str;
return str.replace('&',escape('&'));
return escape(str);
//return escape(str.replace(/%/g, '%25').replace(/\+/g, '%2B')).replace(/%25/g, '%');

id_membre_connected='';
////////////////////////////
favorite_list=false;
get_favoris_list=function(s,show_favoris)
{
if(!s)s='';
var url='channels.php?id_membre='+id_membre_connected+'&get_favoris='+s;
if((favorite_list==true)&&(show_favoris!==true)){favorite_list=false;url='channels.php?id_membre='+id_membre_connected;}
else{favorite_list=true;}
new_ajax(url,function(r){

document.getElementById('listchaine').innerHTML=r;

try{
document.getElementById('favoris_checkbox').checked=favorite_list;
}catch(err){}

});
}
////////////////////////////////////////
del_favoris=function(id_file,name_file,rtmp)
{
try{
new_ajax('favoris.php?del_favoris=1&file='+id_file+'&name='+name_file+'&rtmp='+urlencode(rtmp)+'&id_membre='+id_membre_connected,function(r){
get_favoris_list('',true);
});
}catch(err){}
}
////////////////////////////////////////
set_favoris=function(id_file,name_file,rtmp)
{
try{
new_ajax('favoris.php?add_favoris=1&file='+id_file+'&name='+name_file+'&rtmp='+urlencode(rtmp)+'&id_membre='+id_membre_connected,function(r){
get_favoris_list();
});
}catch(err){}
}
////////////////////////////////////////
add_remove_favoris_list=function()
{
if(!document.getElementById('channel_name_'+curent_number_keyboard)){return;}
var id_file=document.getElementById('channel_name_'+curent_number_keyboard).innerHTML;
var name_file=id_file;
var rtmp=document.getElementById('rtmp_'+curent_number_keyboard).innerHTML;
if(favorite_list==true)
{
del_favoris(id_file,name_file,rtmp);
get_favoris_list('',true);
}
else
{
set_favoris(id_file,name_file,rtmp);
//get_favoris_list('',false);
get_favoris_list('',true);
}
}

<script>
(function() {
	var 
		fullScreenApi = { 
			supportsFullScreen: false,
			isFullScreen: function() { return false; }, 
			requestFullScreen: function() {}, 
			cancelFullScreen: function() {},
			fullScreenEventName: '',
			prefix: ''
		},
		browserPrefixes = 'webkit moz o ms khtml'.split(' ');
	
	// check for native support
	if (typeof document.cancelFullScreen != 'undefined') {
		fullScreenApi.supportsFullScreen = true;
	} else {	 
		// check for fullscreen support by vendor prefix
		for (var i = 0, il = browserPrefixes.length; i < il; i++ ) {
			fullScreenApi.prefix = browserPrefixes[i];
			
			if (typeof document[fullScreenApi.prefix + 'CancelFullScreen' ] != 'undefined' ) {
				fullScreenApi.supportsFullScreen = true;
				
				break;
			}
		}
	}
	
	// update methods to do something useful
	if (fullScreenApi.supportsFullScreen) {
		fullScreenApi.fullScreenEventName = fullScreenApi.prefix + 'fullscreenchange';
		
		fullScreenApi.isFullScreen = function() {
			switch (this.prefix) {	
				case '':
					return document.fullScreen;
				case 'webkit':
					return document.webkitIsFullScreen;
				default:
					return document[this.prefix + 'FullScreen'];
			}
		}
		fullScreenApi.requestFullScreen = function(el) {
			full_screen_on=true;
			return (this.prefix === '') ? el.requestFullScreen() : el[this.prefix + 'RequestFullScreen']();
		}
		fullScreenApi.cancelFullScreen = function(el) {
			full_screen_on=false;
			return (this.prefix === '') ? document.cancelFullScreen() : document[this.prefix + 'CancelFullScreen']();
		}		
	}

	// jQuery plugin
	if (typeof jQuery != 'undefined') {
		jQuery.fn.requestFullScreen = function() {
	
			return this.each(function() {
				var el = jQuery(this);
				if (fullScreenApi.supportsFullScreen) {
					fullScreenApi.requestFullScreen(el);
				}
			});
		};
	}

	// export api
	window.fullScreenApi = fullScreenApi;	
})();
</script>

}

		<span class="tooltip"></span> <!-- Tooltip -->
		<div id="slider"></div> <!-- the Slider -->
		<span class="volume"></span> <!-- Volume -->

	<script src="volume/js/jquery-1.7.2.min.js"></script>
	<script src="volume/js/jquery-ui-1.8.21.custom.min.js"></script>
	<script>
		window.onload=function(){

			//Store frequently elements in variables
			var slider  = $('#slider'),
				tooltip = $('.tooltip');

			//Hide the Tooltip at first
			tooltip.hide();
try{var volume=player.getVolume();}catch(err){var volume=35;}
if(!volume)volume=35;
			//Call the Slider
			slider.slider({
				//Config
				range: "min",
				min: 1,
				value: volume,

				start: function(event,ui) {
				    tooltip.fadeIn('fast');
				},

				//Slider Event
				slide: function(event, ui) { //When the slider is sliding

					var value  = slider.slider('value'),
						volume = $('.volume');

					tooltip.css('left', value).text(ui.value);  //Adjust the tooltip accordingly
try{player.setVolume(ui.value);}catch(err){}
					if(value <= 5) { 
						volume.css('background-position', '0 0');
					} 
					else if (value <= 25) {
						volume.css('background-position', '0 -25px');
					} 
					else if (value <= 75) {
						volume.css('background-position', '0 -50px');
					} 
					else {
						volume.css('background-position', '0 -75px');
					};

				},

				stop: function(event,ui) {
				    tooltip.fadeOut('fast');
				},
			});

		}
	</script><script>
play_pause=function(play,action)
{
var ic=document.getElementById('play_pause_icone');
if(play){
ic.src="http://www.teledunet.com/mobile/play.png";
if(action==true)
player_play();
}
else{
ic.src="http://www.teledunet.com/mobile/pause.png";
if(action==true)
player_play();
}
}
</script>
